    "ever since the discovery of the high proper motion of barnard s star ( @xcite ) , proper motion has proved to be an effective method to identify faint stars in the solar neighborhood .",
    "even thin disk stars , which are comoving with the sun , have residual velocities of the order of tens of kms@xmath1 .",
    "this arises mainly from the fact that , as stars age , they randomly interact with interstellar cloud complexes and spiral arms , which progressively increase their velocity dispersion .",
    "this leads to proper motions of about 100masyr@xmath1 for stars up to @xmath250pc .    with the advent of sensitive near - infrared hybrid mosaic detectors ,",
    "the search for low - mass stars and substellar objects has become possible .",
    "hundreds of ultracool dwarfs ( ucds ; spectral type m7 or later ; @xcite ) have been discovered through large - scale red - optical ( 0.61.0@xmath3 m ) surveys , such as the sloan digital sky survey ( sdss ; @xcite ) , the canada - france brown dwarf survey ( cfbds ; @xcite ) , the pan - starrs1 3@xmath4 survey ( ps1 ; @xcite ) , along with large - scale and all - sky nir ( 1.02.5@xmath3 m ) surveys , e.g.  the deep near infrared survey ( denis ; @xcite ) , the two micron all sky survey ( 2mass ; @xcite ) , the ukirt infrared deep sky survey ( ukidss ; @xcite ) , the vista hemisphere survey ( vhs ; @xcite ) and the all - sky mid - infrared ( 3.422@xmath3 m ) wide - field infrared survey explorer ( wise ; @xcite ) survey .",
    "most of these surveys used color - based criteria to identify ucds ( @xcite , @xcite , @xcite , @xcite , @xcite ) . while this is an effective way of finding ucds",
    ", it may overlook objects with peculiar colors , such as very low metallicity halo objects ( subdwarfs ; @xcite , @xcite ) .",
    "furthermore , an increase in opacity of the ch@xmath5 , h@xmath6o and h@xmath6 molecules in the atmosphere of l / t transition dwarfs ( l6t4.5 ) leads to nir colors similar to those of m and early - l dwarfs ( @xcite , @xcite ) .",
    "the ability to select transition dwarf candidates for spectroscopic follow - up is important to uncover a large sample of these objects and better understand the processes causing condensate cloud disruption ( @xcite , @xcite , @xcite ) , which is known to happen in their photosphere as they evolve and cool down .",
    "this effect has been demonstrated in several variability studies ( @xcite and references therein ) .",
    "while recent studies were able to discover some l / t transition dwarfs ( @xcite , @xcite ) , it is likely that several more are still hiding in surveys such as 2mass and wise .",
    "this could also be said of ucds very close to the sun .",
    "previous studies ( @xcite , @xcite , @xcite , @xcite ) have suggested that the space density of brown dwarfs is below that of stars , with possibly a minimum at the l / t transition ( @xcite and references therein ) .",
    "however , the recent finding of the brown dwarf binary wise  j104915.57@xmath7531906.1 ( @xcite ) , and of the coldest brown dwarf known to date , wise  j085510.83@xmath7071442.5 ( @xcite ) , outclassing wolf 359 and lalande 21185 as the third and fourth closest systems to the sun , provides evidence that the search for ucds in the solar neighborhood is far from over .",
    "the proper motion method is the most efficient way of uncovering nearby ( @xmath8 50pc ) ucds in a color - unbiased search , just as it is for warmer stars .",
    "while some surveys include multi - epoch observations that can lead to a detection of proper motion ( @xcite , @xcite ) , the small timespan ( @xmath212yr ) between individual observations is better suited for the detection of very large proper motions .",
    "this is the case for allwise ( @xcite ) , released to track down high - proper motion objects in the wise catalog .",
    "however , as noted by @xcite , allwise measures only the apparent motion on the sky , because most objects were observed only at two epochs separated by six months .",
    "this interval maximizes the effect of the parallax on the motion of the sources , hindering the calculation of their true proper motion .",
    "some studies have combined the different epochs of two or more of those surveys to search for high proper motion objects : denis and 2mass ( @xcite ) , 2mass and sdss ( @xcite , @xcite , @xcite ) , 2mass and ukidss ( @xcite ) , and more recently 2mass and wise ( @xcite , @xcite ) or 2mass and allwise ( @xcite ) and pan - starrs and allwise ( @xcite ) .",
    "others used several of those surveys to identify new candidates ( @xcite , @xcite ) or added a second epoch of @xmath9 band astrometry , such as the ukidss galactic plane survey ( gps ; @xcite ) , in which a new t5 dwarf and several other l and t dwarf candidates were recently discovered in the galactic plane ( @xcite ) .",
    "it is in this context that the large area near - infrared proper motion survey ( simp ) was initiated using the 2mass point source catalog ( psc ) as a first epoch .",
    "this brings the possibility of discovering ucds in the solar neighborhood that were missed in other searches , such as l / t transition dwarfs or ucds with peculiar photometric colors .",
    "this survey is also suited for the discovery of wide binaries and members of young moving groups .",
    "discovering more of these objects will help constrain the substellar mass function and the brown dwarf space density in the solar neighborhood .",
    "furthermore , cataloging a large number of high - proper motion brown dwarfs will be useful for predicting microlensing events , enabling an independent and direct measurement of their masses ( @xcite ) .    since 2mass and",
    "simp use similar filters and pixel scales and reach photometric comparable depths ( see section  [ simpsurvey ] ) , cross - matching sources is straightforward .",
    "this survey has already enabled the discovery of several ucds : a bright , nearby t2.5 dwarf ( simp  j013656.5 + 093347 ; @xcite ) , five very low - mass binaries ( simp  j1619275 + 031350ab & simp  j1501530@xmath7013506ab ; @xcite , 2mass  j10432513@xmath71706065 , 2mass  j11150150 + 1607026 & 2mass  j12594167 + 1001380 ; @xcite ) and a low - gravity l5  @xmath10 candidate member of the argus association ( simp  j21543454@xmath71055308 ; @xcite , @xcite ) .",
    "this paper presents the remaining ucds discovered so far through the simp survey .",
    "the simp survey is described in detail in section  [ simpsurvey ] , and the spectroscopic and photometric follow - ups are presented in section  [ spectrocand ] and section  [ photoobs ] , respectively .",
    "we describe the method used to classify the candidates in section  [ spectral_class ] and we present the results in section  [ results ] .",
    "we summarize and conclude in section  [ summary ] .",
    "the simp survey was initiated in early 2005 , when a newly developed wide - field near - infrared camera , the camera panoramique proche infra - rouge ( cpapir ; @xcite ) , was installed at the cerro tololo inter - american observatory ( ctio ) 1.5-m telescope , which is operated by the smarts consortium .",
    "cpapir uses a hawaii - ii 2048@xmath112048 hgcdte detector and is designed to image a large portion of the sky at once , making it one of the most efficient nir survey instruments for small - class ( up to 2-m ) telescopes . at the ctio , it has a pixel scale of 103 , yielding a field of view of 348@xmath11348 .",
    "two filter wheels contain 10 broad- and narrow - band filters , within its 0.82.5@xmath3 m bandpass .",
    "cpapir was used at ctio from 2005 february to 2007 march .    from 2007",
    "august to 2009 november , the simp survey was conducted with cpapir at the observatoire du mont - mgantic ( omm ) 1.6-m telescope ( @xcite ) .",
    "the omm and ctio survey procedures were similar ( see below ) , except that the omm field of view decreased to @xmath12 , with a pixel scale of 089 .",
    "the simp observations were obtained in the mko @xmath13 band ( @xmath14 m and @xmath15 m ) for two reasons : ( 1 ) to minimize the sky background level , which is the main source of noise for faint objects , and ( 2 ) to identify the t dwarfs , which have blue @xmath16 colors . at each sky position , 3 to 5 individual 8s exposures were obtained , with a 7@xmath17dither pattern along the declination axis .",
    "the survey was divided in stripes extending over 20 degrees in declination , to minimize telescope dithering time , and it was highly automated with computer scripts .",
    "the number of exposures obtained at each sky position was adjusted in function of the observing conditions to reach a @xmath18 depth of @xmath19 .",
    "figure  [ f1 ] shows the source count as a function of @xmath13 magnitude for both the 2mass and simp photometry of a 6.7 square degree area of the sky corresponding to one night of simp data .",
    "the simp and 2mass source counts agree precisely up to @xmath20 . for @xmath21 ,",
    "the number of sources appears slightly but systematically larger in 2mass than in simp . in the @xmath22 range ,",
    "the simp source count is @xmath23 of the 2mass source count , but a simp counterpart is found for @xmath24 of the 2mass sources in that magnitude range , within 2@xmath17 ( or 1 simp fwhm ) .",
    "the source count discrenpancy is probably due to uncertainties on the magnitudes , and the plot is consistent with the simp source count being complete to @xmath25 .",
    "the simp survey is thus limited by the depth of the 2mass survey .    the simp survey has covered @xmath0 of the sky ; the region surveyed was restricted to absolute galactic latitudes larger than 20(except for a few specifically targeted nearby stars ) to avoid source confusion when cross - matching with 2mass .",
    "the final simp survey contains more than 115 000 raw frames ; a custom idl pipeline was developed to reduce these data . each individual frame",
    "is divided by a flat field image obtained from on and off dome - flats taken either at the beginning or at the end of each night .",
    "a bad pixel mask is applied and a running median of 11 exposures is used to substract sky emission before individual images are median combined .    an astrometric solution is obtained for each simp image based on the 2mass psc , and the simp images are corrected for spatial distortion using a second order polynomial in both directions , in order to minimize the residual errors between the psc and simp positions .",
    "figure  [ f2 ] presents the positional uncertainty in right ascension and declination as a function of @xmath13 magnitude , for the same data subset as in figure  [ f1 ] .",
    "the 2mass uncertainties are plotted as given in the psc .",
    "they amount to @xmath2006 in each direction for @xmath26 , increasing to @xmath202 in each direction at @xmath27 .",
    "the simp curves show the @xmath28 positional uncertainty in ra and dec obtained from the difference in position measured for those sources that were observed twice due to frame overlap .",
    "the simp uncertainties are @xmath2008 in each direction for @xmath26 , increasing to @xmath2011 at @xmath27 .      the simp survey being roughly half a magnitude more sensitive than the typical @xmath29 limit of 2mass , cross - matching between simp and 2mass is done by searching in the simp images for a counterpart to the psc sources that meet the following criteria : they must have a @xmath13-band photometric quality ( ph@xmath30qual ) of a , b , or c , an @xmath31-band photometric quality of a , b , c , or d , they must not be flagged as a minor planet ( mp@xmath30flg = 0 ) , and there must be no confusion ( cc@xmath30flg = 0 ) or galaxy contamination ( gal@xmath30contam = 0 ) .",
    "a match is made with the nearest source in the simp image that is within @xmath32 of the 2mass source , is not already matched to another source , has a profile sharpness consistent with a gaussian , has a long to short axis ratio less than 3 , and is within a matching radius of 27@xmath17 .",
    "the proper motion detection limit of the survey was derived from the astrometric uncertainties in both 2mass and simp .",
    "since 2mass started in 1997 june and ended in 2001 february , the difference in epochs between simp and 2mass varies between 4 and 12 years . for an average timespan of 8 years",
    ", proper motions down to @xmath33 can be measured to @xmath18 for @xmath26 , increasing to @xmath34 at @xmath27 . for the 27@xmath17 matching radius ,",
    "the typical upper bound limit on proper motion is @xmath35 .",
    "the use of a photometric color criterion makes it possible to select ucd candidates with proper motions down to @xmath36 with minimal contamination by other sources . for this purpose",
    ", we used @xmath37-band photometry from the supercosmos sky survey ( sss ; @xcite ) or , if available , @xmath38 photometry from sdss .",
    "if neither of these surveys were available , follow - up @xmath39 and @xmath40-band observations were obtained with megacam ( @xcite ) at the canada - france - hawaii telescope ( cfht ) by taking single 200s exposures .",
    "the megacam photometry is in the ab system , like sdss , and no color - dependent corrections were applied ( see @xcite for photometric corrections from sdss to megacam ) .",
    "the resulting @xmath39 magnitude , for those candidates that were confirmed spectroscopically , is presented in table  [ t5 ] of section  [ results ] .",
    "a target is selected as a candidate for further observation if either one of these criteria is met :    1- @xmath41 and detected in @xmath37 with @xmath42    2- @xmath41 , with a @xmath43 upper limit on @xmath37 ( @xmath44 ) such that @xmath45 .",
    "3- @xmath46 and undetected in @xmath37 .    for",
    "a typical velocity dispersion of @xmath225kms@xmath1 , stars with @xmath41 will be within 50pc of the sun .",
    "dwarfs of type m8v and earlier have @xmath47 and @xmath48 ( @xcite ) .",
    "if such a star were closer than 50pc from the sun , it would be detected in the @xmath37 band and rejected due to its blue @xmath49 color .",
    "nevertheless , some m dwarfs were still selected , as they were found to meet the third criterion ( see section  [ results ] for more detail ) .    in figure  [ f3 ] , the selection criteria are represented as a line on a plot of the @xmath49 color versus proper motion , for ucds discovered in this work , other known ucds with measured @xmath39 magnitude and proper motion , and the simp survey sources from the same data subset as in figure  [ f1 ] . for legibility , ucds with @xmath50 or a @xmath51 are omitted from the graph . for the data subset , the @xmath37-band magnitude was obtained from sss , and if the source is undetected in the @xmath37 band , an @xmath49 color is calculated using the sss survey limit , @xmath52 . for the ucds discovered in this work and other known ucds , the @xmath39-band magnitude was obtained from sdss or megacam when available . as shown in figure  [ f3 ] , for a data subset typical of the whole survey ,",
    "ucd selection criteria eliminate all but 11 candidates among the 27644 simp survey sources . yet , all except one of the ucds identified by other surveys , with measured @xmath53 color and proper motion , satisfy the color criteria . as expected , the simp survey will miss the low proper motion ucds .",
    "a few simp ucds are found outside the selection criteria as their proper motion or color , given in table  [ t5 ] , has been updated with data posterior to the simp survey .",
    "once a considerable list of candidates had been extracted from the simp survey , a spectroscopic follow - up to confirm their ucd nature and determine their spectral type , was conducted at four different telescopes , with as many nir instruments , as described in the following subsections .",
    "limits on telescope time imposed a selection of the candidates to be observed spectroscopically , based on the magnitude of their proper motion , their optical - nir colors , and airmass considerations .",
    "table  [ t1 ] presents a log of all spectroscopic observations , in order of increasing right ascension of the targets .",
    "their 2mass designation is given in column  1 ; hereafter , the coordinate will be abbreviated to the first four digits of the ra and dec ( i.e. simp j23185497@xmath71301106 becomes j2318@xmath71301 ) .",
    "columns  2 - 9 list the instrument used , the ut date of observation , the integration time in minutes , the mode used for the instrument ( when applicable ) , the standard star observed and its spectral type , along with the weather , the mean airmass or any difficulty encountered during the observation .    in total , 197 spectra were obtained for 169 targets . in the next subsections , we detail the observing setups and data reduction processes for every instrument used .",
    "all spectra were corrected for telluric absorption by observing an a - type star immediately before or after the science target .",
    "the spectra of 50 candidates were obtained at the omm 1.6-m telescope during 81 nights , from 2006 april to 2007 november , with the spectromtre infrarouge de montral ( simon ; @xcite ) , featuring a hawaii - i 1024@xmath111024 hgcdte detector with a 046 pixel@xmath1 scale .",
    "all observations were obtained with the amici prism and a 11 wide slit ( 2.4 pixels ) with a north - south orientation , resulting in a spectral resolution @xmath54 over the wavelength range from 0.9@xmath3 m to 2.4@xmath3 m .",
    "the spectra were obtained in series of 9 exposures using a @xmath55 spacing 5-position nod pattern along the slit .",
    "an idl pipeline was used first to divide each image by a flat - field and correct for bad pixels .",
    "sky emission was removed by taking the difference of images obtained at adjacent nod positions .",
    "the spectra were extracted from each difference image , weighted according to their s / n , and combined .",
    "white light recorded through the paschen  @xmath56 or brackett  @xmath57 filters was used for wavelength calibration , in combination with the previously calibrated dispersion of the amici prism .",
    "some spectra having a low - s / n were smoothed using a second order savitzky - golay polynomial filter ( @xcite ) , with a width of 5 points , to help with the visual comparison of the spectra .",
    "spectra for 56 of the fainter simp candidates were obtained at the gemini south telescope from 2006 august to 2007 april with the gemini near - infrared spectrograph ( gnirs ; @xcite ) . the cross - dispersed mode ( xd ) , covering the wavelength range from 0.85@xmath3 m to 2.5@xmath3 m across five orders , was used with the 32 l mm@xmath1 grating and a 03-wide slit , yielding a spectral resolution @xmath58 .",
    "a total of 8 to 33 individual exposures of 60120s were acquired for each target , using a @xmath59 abba nod pattern along the slit .",
    "a custom idl pipeline , detailed in @xcite , was used to reduce all gnirs data . an image acquired with a pinhole mask",
    "is used to correct for the distortion and to straighten up the cross - dispersed spectrum .",
    "pairs of adjacent exposures from the abba pattern are subtracted from each other and the spectra extracted from each difference image are median combined .",
    "the resulting spectrum is wavelength calibrated using an ar lamp , and the calibration is fine - tuned with oh lines from sky emission ( @xcite ) .",
    "observations of 20 of the fainter simp candidates were obtained at the gemini north telescope from 2008 february to 2008 november with the near infrared imager and spectrometer ( niri ; @xcite ) .",
    "the f/6 camera and the 6-pixel ( @xmath207 ) centered slit were used with the krs5 @xmath13 , @xmath31 , and @xmath9 grisms , to obtain a spectral resolution @xmath60 , sufficient to resolve the 1.25@xmath3 m k  i doublet .",
    "the @xmath13 , @xmath31 , and @xmath9 bands of a target spectrum were obtained at different times , and sometimes on different nights , leading to large uncertainties in the relative calibration of the band fluxes . using the 2mass photometry to normalize the fluxes in each band",
    "was also not reliable since the uncertainties on the 2mass photometry for most targets were higher than 0.1 mag .",
    "this led us to normalize each of the @xmath13 , @xmath31 and @xmath9 bands independently to a standard spectrum ( at 1.001.35@xmath3 m , 1.401.80@xmath3 m , and 1.952.40@xmath3 m , respectively ) in order to facilitate the visual classification .",
    "a total of 4 to 30 exposures of 60s were obtained in each band with a @xmath59 nod along the slit .",
    "the reduction pipeline is described in @xcite .",
    "spectroscopic observations of 71 targets were obtained at the nasa infrared telescope facility ( irtf ) for a total of 9 nights grouped in three observing runs , in 2008 february - march , 2008 september , and 2009 april .",
    "the medium - resolution infrared spectrograph spex ( @xcite ) was used either in the cross - dispersed shortxd mode ( sxd , 0.82.46@xmath3 m coverage ) with a 08@xmath1115@xmath61 slit , yielding a spectral resolution @xmath62 , sufficient to resolve the k  i doublet at 1.25@xmath3 m , or in the low - resolution prism mode ( prism , 0.82.5@xmath3 m coverage ) with @xmath63-long slits of width 08 ( @xmath64 ) , 05 ( @xmath65 ) , or 03 ( @xmath66 ) .",
    "the choice of resolution was based on target brightness and observing conditions .",
    "the orientation of the slit was maintained near the parallactic angle .",
    "for each candidate , a total of 6 to 22 exposures of 60240s were acquired using a @xmath67 abba nod pattern along the slit .",
    "the spex data were reduced with version 3.4 of the spextool package ( @xcite ) .",
    "the adjacent image subtraction @xmath68 reduction mode was used together with optimal spectrum extraction ( @xcite ) .",
    "the resulting spectra were wavelength calibrated using ar lamp calibration exposures .",
    "telluric correction and flux calibration were achieved with the _ xtellcor _ procedure that is included in the spextool package ( @xcite ) .",
    "a photometric follow - up in the @xmath13 , @xmath31 and @xmath9 bands was conducted in 2007 and 2008 for 28 targets with low precision 2mass photometry .",
    "these observations were obtained at the omm during the spectroscopic follow - up and simp survey runs , using simon and cpapir respectively , to optimize telescope time when it would allow short photometric measurements , but was insufficient for the longer spectroscopic or survey observations .",
    "the photometry also provided supplementary astrometric epochs to refine the proper motion measurements of our targets .",
    "the raw simon and cpapir images were processed using a custom idl pipeline similar to the simp survey pipeline described in section  [ simpsurvey ] .",
    "aperture photometry was performed , calibrated on 2mass stars in the field of view , while masking the potentially saturated bright stars .",
    "since the nir colors of ucds can vary by up to @xmath20.4 mag depending on the photometric system used ( @xcite ) and the filters in simon and cpapir conform with the mauna kea ( mko ) system ( @xcite ; @xcite ) , the 2mass magnitudes were converted to the mko system using polynomial relations from @xcite .",
    "table  [ t2 ] presents a log of the photometric observations and the results are presented in table  [ t5 ] .",
    "all of the observed spectra were classified by the use of spectral indices as a first step , followed by visual comparison with nir standard spectra , as described in the following subsections .",
    "visual comparison is particularly useful for the low resolution simon spectra , for some low s / n ( @xmath25 ) spectra , and for the identification of peculiar sources such as young or low - metallicity objects , and unresolved binaries .",
    "the spectral indices are most useful when a visual classification is ambiguous .      over the years",
    ", multiple sets of near - infrared spectral indices have been defined to classify ucds .",
    "most of them measure the flux ratio in narrow bands subject to molecular absorption ( h@xmath69o , ch@xmath70 , etc . ) within the @xmath13 , @xmath31 or @xmath9 bands . as any molecular absorption feature varies over a limited range of atmospheric conditions ,",
    "most indices are restricted to a range of spectral types and become inaccurate outside this range .",
    "the broad spectral range of our objects , and the variety of instruments used for this campaign , led to the use of two sets of nir spectral indices .",
    "the first set is made of four indices determined by @xcite to be spectral type sensitive for a broad range of m and l dwarfs while being insensitive to surface gravity .",
    "these indices and their respective valid spectral type range are : h@xmath69o ( m5l4 ) , h@xmath69od ( l0l8 ) , h@xmath69o-1 ( m4l5 ) , and h@xmath69o-2 ( m4l2 ) .",
    "the second set of indices is from @xcite ( with spectral type relations from @xcite ) and is useful for the l and t dwarfs .",
    "these indices and their respective valid spectral type range are : h@xmath69o-@xmath13 ( l0t8 ) , h@xmath69o-@xmath31 ( l0t8 ) , ch@xmath71-@xmath9 ( l0t7 ) , ch@xmath71-@xmath13 ( t0t8 ) , and ch@xmath71-@xmath31 ( t1t8 ) .",
    "table  [ t3 ] lists a compilation of the indices for our targets , along with the calculated spectral type if within the index useful range .",
    "a median type is also given along with its uncertainty , both rounded to the nearest half - integer .",
    "the median type is calculated by iterative rejection of the types ( put in brackets ) that fall too far from the median , until it converges or the rounded uncertainty equals 0.5 .",
    "this resulted in the most likely spectral type from all the useful indices . nevertheless , for some candidates , the indices give a broad range of spectral types or a spectral type that is far from the visual type , due to a lower quality spectrum , or to a peculiar object .",
    "these cases are discussed in section  [ results ] .",
    "the most straightforward and accurate method of classifying stellar spectra is direct comparison with standard spectra ( mk process ; @xcite , @xcite ) .",
    "we therefore compare our @xmath13 , @xmath31 and @xmath9 band spectra with the nir spectral standard sequences listed in table  2 of @xcite , for the t dwarfs , and in table  4 of @xcite , for the m and l dwarfs .",
    "the nir standard spectra extend from 0.7@xmath3 m to 2.5@xmath3 m and they are all available in the spex prism spectral libraries ( @xcite ) , except for m6 and earlier types . for those types , instead of using the nir standards for the comparison , we used the nir spectra of the equivalent optical standards , which are gl 213 ( m4 ) , gl 51 ( m5 ) and gl 406 ( m6 ) . since",
    "only a handful of mid - m dwarfs were found , the use of optical standards should not increase the uncertainties .",
    "we have also used the m6l5 spectral templates defined by @xcite to identify low - gravity ucds , since their set of templates includes both field ( @xmath72 , implied ) and low - gravity ( @xmath56 and @xmath57 ) sequence , extending in the nir the optical sequence of @xcite , which uses the nomenclature scheme introduced by @xcite and @xcite .    the method of choice to assign a spectral type is to visually compare each candidate spectrum with five neighboring spectra of the standard sequence .",
    "the parts of the candidate spectrum that exhibit a very low s / n are masked to avoid interfering with the comparison .",
    "the regions of strong telluric absorption ( 1.151.18@xmath3 m , 1.351.45@xmath3 m and 1.81.95@xmath3 m ) are also masked .",
    "if the candidate and comparison spectra differ in spectral resolution , the higher resolution data are smoothed to the lower resolution .",
    "the candidate and standard spectra are normalized to the same average value over the waveband from 1.235@xmath3 m to 1.305@xmath3 m ( or over the complete range of each individual band in the case of niri spectra ) .",
    "a half - subtype is assigned to a target spectrum when it falls in between two adjacent standard spectra .",
    "following @xcite , the m and l spectra are classified by matching only the @xmath13 band , while the @xmath31 and @xmath9 bands are used to ascertain whether the candidate has a blue or red nir spectrum or one that shows other peculiarities . for the l dwarfs",
    ", the spectral types were also determined by a method developed by k. cruz ( cruz et al .",
    ", in preparation ) that uses , for each optically - anchored spectral type , median - combined spectra reflecting the diversity of spectral morphologies present in each type .",
    "this method visually classifies the spectra using all three nir bands , normalized separately to minimize the difference in nir colors that a given type can display .",
    "the spectral types obtained with both methods agreed within their uncertainties and only the classification with the kirkpatrick method is presented in figure  [ f4 ] .",
    "the visual comparison method yields a typical uncertainty of 1 subtype , although in some cases where the s / n is low or the spectrum displays peculiar features , the uncertainty increases to 2 subtypes . on the other hand ,",
    "if the spectral index method agrees with the visual comparison within 0.5 subtype , and the candidate spectrum matches the standard very closely , the uncertainty of the adopted spectral type is estimated to be 0.5 subtype .",
    "the spectral type of each target , resulting from the classification scheme described in section  [ spectral_class ] is presented in table  [ t4 ] .",
    "the object name is given in column  1 , and a code to the instrument used for the observations is given in column  2 .",
    "results from the observations of an object with different instruments are presented as separate entries .",
    "column  3 gives the spectral type obtained with the spectral indices , column  4 the type obtained from visual comparison , and column  5 the adopted spectral type based on both methods , and weighted according to their respective accuracy .",
    "a `` : '' is used for an adopted spectral type with an uncertainty of @xmath731 subtype , while `` : : '' indicates a larger uncertainty .",
    "spectral types based on previous observations in the optical or the near infrared are also presented in columns  6 and  7 respectively , along with the reference in column  8 .",
    "the spectral type obtained from optical data may differ from the infrared spectral type because the two wavelength ranges probe different layers of the atmosphere and/or because the source is an unresolved binary .",
    "the properties of all targets are presented in table  [ t5 ] , which is subdivided in 8 parts ( normal ucds , young ucds , hyades candidates , unusally red ucds , subdwarf , unusally blue ucds , binary ucds and peculiar ucds ) . in each part , the targets are ordered according to their spectral type ( column  2 ; from column  5 of table  [ t4 ] ) .",
    "the adopted proper motion and its uncertainty are presented in columns 3 and 4 . in order to get the most accurate proper motion possible",
    ", it was recalculated after the simp survey by including the object s position in as many different surveys as available ( column  5 ) .",
    "the different epochs used are from 2mass - psc , simp , sdss - dr9 , cfht follow - up , omm follow - up and allwise . to ensure that every position corresponds to the same moving object at different epochs",
    ", a visual inspection was performed in each survey .",
    "the adopted proper motion is the median of the values obtained in a @xmath74-step monte carlo simulation by linear regression over source positions randomly chosen around the astrometric measurements , according to a gaussian distribution of width equal to each measurement uncertainty .",
    "the standard deviation of the simulated distribution determines the uncertainty on the adopted proper motion .",
    "a photometric distance ( @xmath75~phot~ ) , calculated with the wise @xmath76 band ( or @xmath31 if @xmath76 was unavailable ) and polynomial fits for @xmath77 ( or @xmath78 ) from @xcite , is listed in column  7 .",
    "a tangential velocity ( @xmath79~tan~ ) , derived from the photometric distance and the proper motion , is listed in column  6 .",

    "@xcite suggest to classify as peculiar ( blue or red ) any object whose 1.52.5@xmath3 m continuum is significantly bluer / redder than expected and the cause is not obviously low metallicity for blue objects or low gravity for red objects , whereas @xcite , who did not obtain spectra for the objects studied , used a photometric color criterion only : the 2mass color @xmath82 ( or mko @xmath83 converted to the 2mass system ) must be off by more than @xmath84 from the mean color of known field objects with the same spectral type .",
    "we use both spectral and color information . for an object to be defined as a `` pec red '' or `` pec blue '' , in addition to the 1.52.5@xmath3 m continuum criterion , its 2mass @xmath82 color ( or the mko photometric observations if observed with better precision ) must be off by more than @xmath28 from the mean color of field objects of the same type , as can be seen in figure  [ f5 ] .",
    "objects with a peculiar spectrum but an uncertain color , or objects with a definite abnormal color but an otherwise normal spectrum , are labelled as pec@xmath85 ( possibly red ) or as pec@xmath86 ( possibly blue ) and are discussed in subsection  [ peculiar ] .",
    "young late - m and l dwarfs are still contracting ; they are larger and less massive than older dwarfs of the same spectral type and their spectra display peculiar features , such as weaker alkali and molecular absorption lines , a flatter 2.182.28@xmath3 m continuum and a triangular - shaped continuum in the @xmath31 band due to a decrease of collision - induced absorption of molecular hydrogen , as a consequence of their low gravity .",
    "the properties of the young candidates found in the simp survey are presented in table  [ t5]b . as displayed in figure  [ f6 ] ,",
    "their spectra were compared with nir spectral templates of the @xmath56 ( intermediate - gravity ) and @xmath57 ( very low - gravity ) classes for m and l dwarfs , constructed by cruz et al .",
    "( in preparation ) and @xcite .",
    "this visual comparison alone was used to identify an object as a young candidate .",

    "the simp survey recovered three objects that were previously identified as candidate members of the hyades cluster , which has an estimated age of 625@xmath7350myr ( @xcite ) .",
    "while this is young compared to the sun and field stars in general , it makes the hyades older than about 85% of the open clusters in the solar neighborhood ( @xcite ) .",
    "the age of the hyades is much higher than the age estimate for the @xmath88 gravity - class ( log(age ) ( yr ) @xmath90 7 ) , and even at the higher limit of the age estimate of the @xmath91 class ( log(age ) ( yr ) @xmath90 8)(@xcite ) .",
    "the space motion of the hyades cluster members is consistent with parallel motion with an internal velocity dispersion of @xmath92kms@xmath93 ( @xcite ) , and an important test of cluster membership is provided by the comparison of a candidate simp proper motion with the cluster convergence point ( cp ) and velocity .",
    "figure  [ f7 ] shows the proper motion trajectories of stars selected as members of the hyades by @xcite , as calculated from their hipparcos proper motion ( @xcite ) , giving a good measure of the location and extent of the area of convergence .",
    "superimposed on this plot are the trajectories of the three simp hyades cluster candidates , discussed below .",
    "the cluster velocity divided by the magnitude of a candidate proper motion gives its kinematic distance ( @xmath75~kin~ ; @xcite ) .",
    "the hyades cluster has a tidal radius of 10pc and a central distance of 46.34@xmath730.27pc ( @xcite ) and a better test of membership may result from a comparison of the kinematic distance with the photometric distance ( column  7 of table  [ t5 ] ) than with the cluster central distance .",

    "subdwarfs are ucds with a low metallicity and a higher surface gravity and atmospheric pressure .",
    "this causes an increase of the collision - induced absorption ( cia ) by h@xmath6 in the @xmath31 and @xmath9 bands , hence an unusually blue @xmath101 color .",
    "they also have stronger hydride bands ( cah , crh , feh ) , since the metal - metal molecules ( tio , vo ) are less abundant , leaving the absorption by hydride molecules more prominent .",
    "metal ( ti i and ca i ) and alkali ( na i , k i , cs i and rb i ) lines also remain important at lower temperatures since condensate formation is delayed due to the less frequent interactions of the rarefied atoms . finally , as part of the galactic halo",
    ", they move with high transverse velocities ( @xmath111kms@xmath93 ) and are easily detectable in proper motion surveys .",
    "one such object , j1158@xmath810435 , was recovered in the simp survey .",
    "this blue ( @xmath112 ) , very high proper motion object has an adopted spectral type of sdl7@xmath732 , its spectrum displaying strongly suppressed @xmath31 and @xmath9 bands and a strong feh band around 1.24@xmath3 m .",
    "this subdwarf was first identified by @xcite as an l3 candidate through sdss colors .",
    "our result agrees with the sdl7 classification by @xcite , based on both optical and nir spectra .",
    "objects having a 2mass @xmath82 color significantly bluer than the color of field ucds ( see figure  [ f5 ] ) , and a 1.52.5@xmath3 m continuum significantly bluer than the best - matching field standard , while not showing obvious signs of low metallicity such as hydride bands , are classified as peculiar ( blue ) and are presented in table  [ t5]f .",

    "the follow - up of our candidates revealed several spectra displaying peculiarities that could be attributed to the combined emission from two unresolved ucds .",
    "in particular , the combined spectrum of a t dwarf and an earlier - type ucd features bumps where the flux of the t dwarf emerges between the strong h@xmath150o and ch@xmath151 absorption bands , the most prominent being around @xmath152 m .",
    "we searched for such binaries in our sample using the visual inspection method described in @xcite , which combines spectra from the spex library and performs a chi - square per degree of freedom fit to see if the combination of two spectral types results in a better match than any single object spectrum .",
    "this section presents the cases where a two - object combination yields a better match to the observed spectrum , but we emphasize that these sources remain binary candidates until this hypothesis is confirmed either by high - resolution imaging or a radial velocity follow - up .",
    "this is especially the case for j0006@xmath71319 and j0006@xmath70852 , where the t dwarf spectrum is at the noise level , leading to a small ( @xmath1531 ) chi - square .",
    "the adopted spectral types listed in table  [ t4 ] take into account the comparison with a two - object combination , as seen figure  [ f9 ] , while the visual classification listed in the same table is based only on comparison with single standards .    _",

    "a sample of 169 spectra have been obtained from different observatories for ucd candidates found through proper motion detection by comparing source position from the simp survey to 2mass . from this sample , 164 ucds , with spectral type from m8 to t6.5 , were found , including 2 young field brown dwarfs , 6 unusually red m and l dwarfs , 25 unusually blue m and l dwarfs , 2 candidate unresolved l+t binaries and 24 other peculiar ucds .",
    "we also discovered 18 l / t transition dwarfs ( l6-t4.5 ) , which helps better populate this interesting range of spectral type , often the target of variability studies .",
    "this work demonstrates that many undiscovered ucds remain to be found in preexisting surveys , including several peculiar objects .",
    "proper motion has proved to be an efficient method to uncover those missed objects . furthermore , most objects found are relatively bright ( @xmath173 ) , enabling follow - up studies ( parallax , variability , binarity , etc . ) .",

    "<S> we have conducted a near - infrared ( nir ) proper motion survey , the _ sondage infrarouge de mouvement propre _ ( simp ) , in order to discover field ultracool dwarfs ( ucd ) in the solar neighborhood . </S>",
    "<S> the survey was conducted by imaging @xmath0 of the sky with the camera panoramique proche - infrarouge ( cpapir ) both in the southern hemisphere at the cerro tololo inter - american observatory ( ctio ) 1.5-m telescope , and in the northern hemisphere at the observatoire du mont - mgantic ( omm ) 1.6-m telescope and comparing the source positions from these observations with the two micron all - sky survey point source catalog ( 2mass psc ) . </S>",
    "<S> additional color criteria were used to further discriminate unwanted astrophysical sources . </S>",
    "<S> we present the results of a nir spectroscopic follow - up of 169 m , l and t dwarfs . among the sources discovered are two young field brown dwarfs , six unusually red m and l dwarfs , twenty - five unusually blue m and l dwarfs , two candidate unresolved l+t binaries and twenty - four peculiar ucds . </S>",
    "<S> additionally , we add nine l / t transition dwarfs ( l6t4.5 ) to the already known objects . </S>"
